<p><b>Kevin De Bruyne</b> (<small>Dutch pronunciation:&#32;</small><span title="Representation in the International Phonetic Alphabet (IPA)" class="IPA"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Dutch" title="Help:IPA/Dutch">[kvn d brœyn]</a></span>; born 28 June 1991) is a Belgian professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder" title="Midfielder">midfielder</a> for <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> club <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a>, where he is vice-captain, and the <a href="/wiki/Belgium_national_football_team" title="Belgium national football team">Belgian national team</a>. Recognized for his exceptional passing, shooting and dribbling abilities, he is widely considered to be one of the best players in the world and has often been described as a "complete" midfielder. 
</p><p>De Bruyne began his career at <a href="/wiki/K.R.C._Genk" title="K.R.C. Genk">Genk</a>, where he was a regular player when they won the <a href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%9311_Belgian_Pro_League" title="2010–11 Belgian Pro League">2010–11 Belgian Pro League</a>. In 2012, he joined English club <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a>, where he was used sparingly and then loaned to <a href="/wiki/SV_Werder_Bremen" title="SV Werder Bremen">Werder Bremen</a>. He signed with <a href="/wiki/VfL_Wolfsburg" title="VfL Wolfsburg">Wolfsburg</a> for £18 million in 2014, where he established himself as one of the best players in the <a href="/wiki/Bundesliga" title="Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a> and was integral in the club's <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_DFB-Pokal" title="2014–15 DFB-Pokal">2014–15 DFB-Pokal</a> win. In the summer of 2015, De Bruyne joined Manchester City for a club record £54 million. He has since won two Premier League titles, four <a href="/wiki/EFL_Cup" title="EFL Cup">League Cups</a> and an <a href="/wiki/FA_Cup" title="FA Cup">FA Cup</a> with the club. In <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Premier_League" title="2017–18 Premier League">2017–18</a>, he had a significant role in Manchester City's record in becoming the only Premier League team to <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_records_and_statistics#Points" title="Premier League records and statistics">attain 100 points</a> in a single season. In <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Premier_League" title="2019–20 Premier League">2019–20</a>, De Bruyne tied the record for most assists in a Premier League season and was awarded <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_Player_of_the_Season" title="Premier League Player of the Season">Player of the Season</a>.
</p><p>De Bruyne made his full international debut in 2010, and he has since earned 78 <a href="/wiki/Caps_(football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Caps (football)">caps</a> and scored 20 goals for Belgium. He was a member of the Belgian squads that reached the quarter-finals both at the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a> and at <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">UEFA Euro 2016</a>. He represented Belgium at the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a>, where Belgium won the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup#Third_place_play-off" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">third place play-off</a> match against <a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team" title="England national football team">England</a>, and was named in the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup_awards#All-Star_Team" title="FIFA World Cup awards">FIFA World Cup Dream Team</a>.
</p><p>De Bruyne has been named in the <a href="/wiki/International_Federation_of_Football_History_%26_Statistics#IFFHS_Men&#39;s_World_Team" title="International Federation of Football History &amp; Statistics">IFFHS Men's World Team</a>, the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Team_of_the_Year" title="UEFA Team of the Year">UEFA Team of the Year</a> and the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> Squad of the Season three times each, the <a href="/wiki/European_Sports_Magazines#ESM_Team_of_the_Year" class="mw-redirect" title="European Sports Magazines">ESM Team of the Year</a> twice, the <i><a href="/wiki/France_Football" title="France Football">France Football</a></i> World XI, and the Bundesliga Team of the Year. He won the <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_Playmaker_of_the_Season" title="Premier League Playmaker of the Season">Premier League Playmaker of the Season</a> twice, <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City#Player_of_the_Year" class="mw-redirect" title="Manchester City">Manchester City's Player of the Season</a> three times, the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Players%27_Player_of_the_Year" title="PFA Players&#39; Player of the Year">PFA Players' Player of the Year</a>, the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Club_Football_Awards#Best_Midfielder" title="UEFA Club Football Awards">UEFA Champions League Midfielder of the Season</a>, the Bundesliga Player of the Year, the <a href="/wiki/Footballer_of_the_Year_(Germany)" title="Footballer of the Year (Germany)">Footballer of the Year (Germany)</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Belgian_Sportsman_of_the_year" title="Belgian Sportsman of the year">Belgian Sportsman of the Year</a> and the <a href="/wiki/International_Federation_of_Football_History_%26_Statistics#IFFHS_World&#39;s_Best_Man_Playmaker" title="International Federation of Football History &amp; Statistics">IFFHS World's Best Playmaker</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kevin_De_Bruyne&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Genk">Genk</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kevin_De_Bruyne&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Genk">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>De Bruyne began his career with hometown club KVV Drongen in 1997. Two years later, he joined <a href="/wiki/K.A.A._Gent" title="K.A.A. Gent">Gent</a> and moved to <a href="/wiki/K.R.C._Genk" title="K.R.C. Genk">Genk</a> in 2005. De Bruyne continued his development in their youth set-up and was rewarded for his progress by being promoted to the first team squad in 2008. From an Interview with his youth club, it was revealed that De Bruyne was a <a href="/wiki/Liverpool" title="Liverpool">Liverpool</a> fan and admirer of <a href="/wiki/Michael_Owen" title="Michael Owen">Michael Owen</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>De Bruyne made his first team debut for <a href="/wiki/K.R.C._Genk" title="K.R.C. Genk">Genk</a> in a 3–0 defeat at <a href="/wiki/S._du_Pays_de_Charleroi" class="mw-redirect" title="S. du Pays de Charleroi">Charleroi</a> on 9 May 2009.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> Having established himself in the team <a href="/wiki/2009%E2%80%9310_Belgian_Pro_League" title="2009–10 Belgian Pro League">the following season</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-NFT_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NFT-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> on 7 February 2010, De Bruyne scored his first goal for the club, which secured all three points for Genk in a 1–0 win against <a href="/wiki/Standard_Li%C3%A8ge" title="Standard Liège">Standard Liège</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> He scored five goals and made 16 assists in 32 league matches during the 2010–11 season as Genk were crowned <a href="/wiki/Belgian_Pro_League" class="mw-redirect" title="Belgian Pro League">Belgian</a> champions for the third time.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> On 29 October 2011, De Bruyne scored his first hat-trick for Genk against <a href="/wiki/Club_Brugge_K.V." class="mw-redirect" title="Club Brugge K.V.">Club Brugge</a>, which ended in a 5–4 win for Genk.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> On 28 January 2012, De Bruyne scored a brace against <a href="/wiki/Oud-Heverlee_Leuven" title="Oud-Heverlee Leuven">OH Leuven</a> in a 5–0 win. On 18 February 2012, De Bruyne scored his first goal back at Genk following his agreed transfer to <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> and also assisted the other goal in a 1–2 away win against <a href="/wiki/R.A.E.C._Mons" title="R.A.E.C. Mons">Mons</a>. De Bruyne ended the season by wrapping up the scoring in a 3–1 victory over <a href="/wiki/K.A.A._Gent" title="K.A.A. Gent">Gent</a>. He finished the league campaign with eight goals from 28 appearances.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Chelsea">Chelsea</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kevin_De_Bruyne&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Chelsea">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:102px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Kevin_De_Bruyne_Chelsea_vs_AS-Roma_10AUG2013.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Kevin_De_Bruyne_Chelsea_vs_AS-Roma_10AUG2013.jpg/100px-Kevin_De_Bruyne_Chelsea_vs_AS-Roma_10AUG2013.jpg" decoding="async" width="100" height="258" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Kevin_De_Bruyne_Chelsea_vs_AS-Roma_10AUG2013.jpg/150px-Kevin_De_Bruyne_Chelsea_vs_AS-Roma_10AUG2013.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/19/Kevin_De_Bruyne_Chelsea_vs_AS-Roma_10AUG2013.jpg/200px-Kevin_De_Bruyne_Chelsea_vs_AS-Roma_10AUG2013.jpg 2x" data-file-width="570" data-file-height="1470" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Kevin_De_Bruyne_Chelsea_vs_AS-Roma_10AUG2013.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>De Bruyne warming up with Chelsea in 2013</div></div></div>
<p>On 31 January 2012, on the winter transfer deadline day, <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> club Chelsea and Genk announced the permanent signing of De Bruyne, with the fee rumoured to be in the region of £7 million.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> He signed a five-and-a-half-year contract at <a href="/wiki/Stamford_Bridge_(stadium)" title="Stamford Bridge (stadium)">Stamford Bridge</a>, but would stay at Genk for the remainder of the 2011–12 season. De Bruyne told the club website, "To come to a team like Chelsea is a dream but now I have to work hard to achieve the level that's necessary."<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> On 18 July 2012, De Bruyne made his debut for Chelsea in a friendly match against <a href="/wiki/Major_League_Soccer" title="Major League Soccer">Major League Soccer</a> (MLS) side <a href="/wiki/Seattle_Sounders_FC" title="Seattle Sounders FC">Seattle Sounders FC</a> in a 4–2 win. De Bruyne also played the first half against <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1" title="Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a> giants <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a> at <a href="/wiki/Yankee_Stadium" title="Yankee Stadium">Yankee Stadium</a>, <a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">New York</a>.
</p>
<h4><span id="Werder_Bremen_.28loan.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Werder_Bremen_(loan)">Werder Bremen (loan)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kevin_De_Bruyne&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Werder Bremen (loan)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:177px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Kevin_de_bruyne_werder.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cc/Kevin_de_bruyne_werder.JPG/175px-Kevin_de_bruyne_werder.JPG" decoding="async" width="175" height="217" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cc/Kevin_de_bruyne_werder.JPG/263px-Kevin_de_bruyne_werder.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/c/cc/Kevin_de_bruyne_werder.JPG 2x" data-file-width="284" data-file-height="352" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Kevin_de_bruyne_werder.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>De Bruyne during his spell with Werder Bremen in 2012</div></div></div>
<p>On 31 July 2012, Chelsea announced that De Bruyne was to join <a href="/wiki/SV_Werder_Bremen" title="SV Werder Bremen">Werder Bremen</a> in the <a href="/wiki/Bundesliga" title="Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a> on a season-long loan deal.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> He scored his first goal for Bremen in a 3–2 defeat to <a href="/wiki/Hannover_96" title="Hannover 96">Hannover 96</a> on 15 September, netting from 11 yards out after being played in by <a href="/wiki/Eljero_Elia" title="Eljero Elia">Eljero Elia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> He continued his good form, scoring in Bremen's next game, a 2–2 draw with <a href="/wiki/VfB_Stuttgart" title="VfB Stuttgart">VfB Stuttgart</a>, on 23 September.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> De Bruyne got back on the score sheet on 18 November, scoring the winning goal — despite his team being down to 10 men — as Bremen came from a goal down to defeat <a href="/wiki/Fortuna_D%C3%BCsseldorf" title="Fortuna Düsseldorf">Fortuna Düsseldorf</a> 2–1.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>De Bruyne scored his first goal in over two months on 4 May 2013, since netting a consolation goal in <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a>'s 6–1 hammering of Bremen, putting his side up 2–0 at home to <a href="/wiki/TSG_1899_Hoffenheim" title="TSG 1899 Hoffenheim">TSG 1899 Hoffenheim</a> before a late brace from <a href="/wiki/Sven_Schipplock" title="Sven Schipplock">Sven Schipplock</a> meant that the game finished 2–2.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> He followed this up with a goal in Bremen's next match, securing a place in the Bundesliga for the next season with a 1–1 draw against <a href="/wiki/Eintracht_Frankfurt" title="Eintracht Frankfurt">Eintracht Frankfurt</a> on 11 May.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Return_to_Chelsea">Return to Chelsea</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kevin_De_Bruyne&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Return to Chelsea">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After a successful loan spell in the Bundesliga with Werder Bremen, De Bruyne was linked with a move to stay in Germany with either <a href="/wiki/Borussia_Dortmund" title="Borussia Dortmund">Borussia Dortmund</a> or <a href="/wiki/Bayer_04_Leverkusen" title="Bayer 04 Leverkusen">Bayer Leverkusen</a>. Incoming manager <a href="/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Mourinho" title="José Mourinho">José Mourinho</a>, however, assured De Bruyne he was a part of Chelsea's plan for the future, and the player officially returned to Chelsea on 1 July 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>De Bruyne injured a knee while scoring his first goal for Chelsea, in a pre-season friendly game against a Malaysia XI,<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> but was fit to make his competitive debut on the opening day of the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_Premier_League" title="2013–14 Premier League">2013–14 Premier League</a> season against <a href="/wiki/Hull_City_A.F.C." title="Hull City A.F.C.">Hull City</a>, and made an assist for the first goal in a 2–0 win.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wolfsburg">Wolfsburg</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kevin_De_Bruyne&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Wolfsburg">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2013.E2.80.9314_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2013–14_season">2013–14 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kevin_De_Bruyne&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 2013–14 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 18 January 2014, <a href="/wiki/VfL_Wolfsburg" title="VfL Wolfsburg">Wolfsburg</a> signed De Bruyne for a fee of £18 million (€22 million).<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> On 25 January 2014, he made his debut for Wolfsburg in a 3–1 home loss against <a href="/wiki/Hannover_96" title="Hannover 96">Hannover 96</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> On 12 April 2014, De Bruyne assisted 2 goals in their 4–1 home win against <a href="/wiki/1._FC_N%C3%BCrnberg" title="1. FC Nürnberg">1. FC Nürnberg</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> After a week he scored his first goal for Wolfsburg in 3–1 away win against <a href="/wiki/Hamburger_SV" title="Hamburger SV">Hamburger SV</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> He also scored in the last two matches of the <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_Bundesliga" title="2013–14 Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a> helping his team to win against <a href="/wiki/VfB_Stuttgart" title="VfB Stuttgart">VfB Stuttgart</a> and <a href="/wiki/Borussia_M%C3%B6nchengladbach" title="Borussia Mönchengladbach">Borussia Mönchengladbach</a>.
</p>
<h4><span id="2014.E2.80.9315_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2014–15_season">2014–15 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kevin_De_Bruyne&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: 2014–15 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Emirates_Cup_-_Arsenal_v_Wolfsburg_(20011199918).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/27/Emirates_Cup_-_Arsenal_v_Wolfsburg_%2820011199918%29.jpg/220px-Emirates_Cup_-_Arsenal_v_Wolfsburg_%2820011199918%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="152" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/27/Emirates_Cup_-_Arsenal_v_Wolfsburg_%2820011199918%29.jpg/330px-Emirates_Cup_-_Arsenal_v_Wolfsburg_%2820011199918%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/27/Emirates_Cup_-_Arsenal_v_Wolfsburg_%2820011199918%29.jpg/440px-Emirates_Cup_-_Arsenal_v_Wolfsburg_%2820011199918%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3698" data-file-height="2559" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Emirates_Cup_-_Arsenal_v_Wolfsburg_(20011199918).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>De Bruyne playing for Wolfsburg against <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a> in July 2015</div></div></div>
<p>De Bruyne scored his first goal of the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_VfL_Wolfsburg_season" title="2014–15 VfL Wolfsburg season">2014–15 season</a> on 2 October 2014, volleying in a clearance from outside the box to salvage a 1–1 draw against <a href="/wiki/LOSC_Lille_M%C3%A9tropole" class="mw-redirect" title="LOSC Lille Métropole">Lille</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2014-15_UEFA_Europa_League" class="mw-redirect" title="2014-15 UEFA Europa League">Europa League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> In the third group match away to <a href="/wiki/FC_Krasnodar" title="FC Krasnodar">Krasnodar</a> on 23 October, De Bruyne scored twice as Wolfsburg secured their first win in the competition with a 4–2 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> On 30 January 2015, he scored another brace in a 4–1 home win against Bayern Munich, their first Bundesliga defeat since April 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-VfL_Wolfsburg_4_1_Bayern_Mun_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-VfL_Wolfsburg_4_1_Bayern_Mun-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> On 1 March 2015, De Bruyne assisted three goals in a 5–3 win over his former club Werder Bremen.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 12 March 2015, De Bruyne scored two goals in a 3–1 first leg Europa League round of 16 victory over <a href="/wiki/Inter_Milan" title="Inter Milan">Internazionale</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> On 15 March 2015, he scored one goal and assisted another two in 3–0 victory over <a href="/wiki/SC_Freiburg" title="SC Freiburg">SC Freiburg</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>De Bruyne ended the league season with 10 goals and 19 assists, the latter a new <a href="/wiki/Bundesliga_records#Assists" class="mw-redirect" title="Bundesliga records">Bundesliga record</a>, as Wolfsburg finished second in the <a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Bundesliga" title="2014–15 Bundesliga">Bundesliga</a> and qualified for the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2015–16 UEFA Champions League">2015–16 UEFA Champions League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup><sup id="ref_N1_1" class="reference"><a href="#cnote_N1">[N1]</a></sup> On 30 May 2015, he started and scored in the <a href="/wiki/2015_DFB-Pokal_Final" title="2015 DFB-Pokal Final">2015 DFB-Pokal Final</a> as <i>Die Wölfe</i> defeated <a href="/wiki/Borussia_Dortmund" title="Borussia Dortmund">Borussia Dortmund</a> 3–1 at the <a href="/wiki/Olympiastadion_(Berlin)" title="Olympiastadion (Berlin)">Olympiastadion</a> in <a href="/wiki/Berlin" title="Berlin">Berlin</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>De Bruyne ended his breakout season with 16 goals and 26 assists in all competitions,<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> and was named the 2015 <a href="/wiki/Footballer_of_the_Year_(Germany)" title="Footballer of the Year (Germany)">Germany Footballer of the Year</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Sporza_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sporza-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2015.E2.80.9316_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2015–16_season">2015–16 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kevin_De_Bruyne&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 2015–16 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>De Bruyne began the season by winning the <a href="/wiki/2015_DFL-Supercup" title="2015 DFL-Supercup">2015 DFL-Supercup</a> against <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a>, providing the cross for <a href="/wiki/Nicklas_Bendtner" title="Nicklas Bendtner">Nicklas Bendtner</a>'s 89th-minute equaliser for a 1–1 draw and then scoring in the subsequent <a href="/wiki/Penalty_shoot-out_(association_football)" title="Penalty shoot-out (association football)">penalty shootout</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-supercup_42-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-supercup-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> On 8 August 2015, he continued his good form by scoring his first goal of the season, and providing two assists in a 4–1 win at <a href="/wiki/Stuttgarter_Kickers" title="Stuttgarter Kickers">Stuttgarter Kickers</a> in the first round of the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_DFB-Pokal" title="2015–16 DFB-Pokal">DFB-Pokal</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In August, De Bruyne, in the midst of transfer speculation, stated that he would not force Wolfsburg to sell him, but also said that he could not ignore interest from <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a>, saying: "If an offer does come, I will hear about it and how much it is, but I have not yet heard anything... I would not go to England just to prove that I can play there. I do not have to go to England... If I go there it's because for me and for my family it is a good choice. That's the key for me."<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 10 August, it was reported that Manchester City had made a second bid for De Bruyne worth £47 million. Wolfsburg sporting director, <a href="/wiki/Klaus_Allofs" title="Klaus Allofs">Klaus Allofs</a>, stated that the club would fight to keep him, saying "I think some other clubs have definitely turned Kevin’s head... Some huge figures are doing the rounds and I can understand why Kevin is leaving everything open."<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 27 August, it was reported that Manchester City had made a bid for De Bruyne worth £58 million. Klaus Allofs said that City had made an "astonishing" wage offer to De Bruyne.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Manchester_City">Manchester City</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kevin_De_Bruyne&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Manchester City">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2015.E2.80.9316_season_2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2015–16_season_2">2015–16 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kevin_De_Bruyne&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: 2015–16 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:187px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Kevin_De_Bruyne_(24640482031)_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Kevin_De_Bruyne_%2824640482031%29_%28cropped%29.jpg/185px-Kevin_De_Bruyne_%2824640482031%29_%28cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="185" height="268" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Kevin_De_Bruyne_%2824640482031%29_%28cropped%29.jpg/278px-Kevin_De_Bruyne_%2824640482031%29_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Kevin_De_Bruyne_%2824640482031%29_%28cropped%29.jpg/370px-Kevin_De_Bruyne_%2824640482031%29_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1089" data-file-height="1580" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Kevin_De_Bruyne_(24640482031)_(cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>De Bruyne playing for <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Man City</a> in January 2016.</div></div></div>
<p>On 30 August 2015, Manchester City announced the arrival of De Bruyne on a six-year contract, for a reported club-record fee of £55 million (€75 million), making him the second most expensive transfer in British football history after <a href="/wiki/%C3%81ngel_Di_Mar%C3%ADa" title="Ángel Di María">Ángel Di María</a>'s move to <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> in 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> He made his debut for the team in the Premier League on 12 September against <a href="/wiki/Crystal_Palace_F.C." title="Crystal Palace F.C.">Crystal Palace</a>, replacing injured <a href="/wiki/Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero" title="Sergio Agüero">Sergio Agüero</a> in the 25th minute.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> On 19 September, he scored his first goal for the club against <a href="/wiki/West_Ham_United_F.C." title="West Ham United F.C.">West Ham United</a> in first half stoppage time in an eventual 2–1 loss.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> He went on to score in a 4–1 <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Football_League_Cup" title="2015–16 Football League Cup">League Cup</a> win against <a href="/wiki/Sunderland_A.F.C." title="Sunderland A.F.C.">Sunderland</a>, on 22 September<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> and a 4–1 loss to <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a> in the Premier League on 26 September.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> On 3 October, he scored in the team's 6–1 win against <a href="/wiki/Newcastle_United_F.C." title="Newcastle United F.C.">Newcastle United</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 2 October, De Bruyne was announced as one of the players on the longlist for the prestigious <a href="/wiki/FIFA_Ballon_d%27Or" title="FIFA Ballon d&#39;Or">FIFA Ballon d'Or</a> award, alongside such teammates as Sergio Agüero and <a href="/wiki/Yaya_Tour%C3%A9" title="Yaya Touré">Yaya Touré</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> Just 18 days later, on 20 October he was revealed by <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a> as one of the players on the 23-man shortlist for the Ballon d'Or.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> On 21 October, De Bruyne scored an injury-time winner against <a href="/wiki/Sevilla_FC" title="Sevilla FC">Sevilla</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2015–16 UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a>, to take City within one point of group leaders <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a>, with three games remaining.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> On 1 December, he scored a brace in a 4–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Hull_City_A.F.C." title="Hull City A.F.C.">Hull City</a> to send Manchester City through to the semi-finals of the Football League Cup.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>
On 27 January 2016, De Bruyne scored a goal in a League Cup semi-final 3–1 victory over <a href="/wiki/Everton_F.C." title="Everton F.C.">Everton</a>, but sustained an injury to his right knee that would keep him out of the team for two months.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> On 2 April, De Bruyne made his return from injury in a 4–0 win against <a href="/wiki/A.F.C._Bournemouth" class="mw-redirect" title="A.F.C. Bournemouth">Bournemouth</a> at <a href="/wiki/Dean_Court" title="Dean Court">Dean Court</a>, scoring the team's second goal in the twelfth minute.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> Four days later, he scored the opening goal in a 2–2 draw with <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase#Quarter-finals" title="2015–16 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">UEFA Champions League quarter-final</a> first-leg at the <a href="/wiki/Parc_des_Princes" title="Parc des Princes">Parc des Princes</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> On 12 April, De Bruyne scored the winning goal against Paris Saint-Germain, advancing Manchester City to the Champions League semi-finals, for the first time in the club's history, on an aggregate score of 3–2. Writing in <i><a href="/wiki/The_Independent" title="The Independent">The Independent</a></i>, Mark Ogden said, "It was a stunning goal from the Belgian, who took a touch to control the ball before curling it beyond <a href="/wiki/Kevin_Trapp" title="Kevin Trapp">Kevin Trapp</a> from the edge of the penalty area."<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> De Bruyne's next goal came on 8 May 2016 in a 2–2 draw with <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a>, although the result left City's Champions League qualification hopes out of their own hands.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup></p><div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Kevin_de_Bruyne_2016-12-26_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/Kevin_de_Bruyne_2016-12-26_%28cropped%29.jpg/200px-Kevin_de_Bruyne_2016-12-26_%28cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="200" height="233" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/Kevin_de_Bruyne_2016-12-26_%28cropped%29.jpg/300px-Kevin_de_Bruyne_2016-12-26_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/23/Kevin_de_Bruyne_2016-12-26_%28cropped%29.jpg/399px-Kevin_de_Bruyne_2016-12-26_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="808" data-file-height="943" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Kevin_de_Bruyne_2016-12-26_(cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>De Bruyne during a match against <a href="/wiki/Hull_City_A.F.C." title="Hull City A.F.C.">Hull City</a> on 26 December 2016.</div></div></div>
<h4><span id="2016.E2.80.9317_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2016–17_season">2016–17 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kevin_De_Bruyne&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: 2016–17 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:33%; ;"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1012376600">.mw-parser-output .quotebox{background-color:#F9F9F9;border:1px solid #aaa;box-sizing:border-box;padding:10px;font-size:88%;max-width:100%}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft{margin:0.5em 1.4em 0.8em 0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright{margin:0.5em 0 0.8em 1.4em}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.centered{margin:0.5em auto 0.8em auto}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft p,.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright p{font-style:inherit}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-title{background-color:#F9F9F9;text-align:center;font-size:larger;font-weight:bold}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:before{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" “ ";vertical-align:-45%;line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:after{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" ” ";line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .left-aligned{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .right-aligned{text-align:right}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .center-aligned{text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .quotebox cite{display:block;font-style:normal}@media screen and (max-width:640px){.mw-parser-output .quotebox{width:100%!important;margin:0 0 0.8em!important;float:none!important}}</style>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"I think he is a special, outstanding player. He makes everything. Without the ball he is the first fighter, and with the ball he is clear – he sees absolutely everything."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">—<a href="/wiki/Pep_Guardiola" title="Pep Guardiola">Pep Guardiola</a> on 17 September 2016 describing De Bruyne after his brilliant performances for City<sup id="cite_ref-skysports.com_63-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-skysports.com-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div><p>
On 10 September 2016, De Bruyne scored and assisted in the first <a href="/wiki/Manchester_derby" title="Manchester derby">Manchester derby</a> of the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_Premier_League" title="2016–17 Premier League">season</a> which City won 2–1 and was awarded the <i>Man of the Match</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> On 17 September 2016, De Bruyne was awarded the <i>Man of the Match</i>, in a 4–0 win over Bournemouth. De Bruyne scored the first, assisted the fourth, and provided key passes on both the second and third goals.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> After the international break, Manchester City drew their next game, against Everton, played on 15 October 2016 with the scoreline finishing at 1–1. <a href="/wiki/Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero" title="Sergio Agüero">Agüero</a> and De Bruyne both missed their penalties while <a href="/wiki/Nolito" title="Nolito">Nolito</a> came off the bench to equalise for City.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> On 1 November, De Bruyne scored from a <a href="/wiki/Direct_free_kick" class="mw-redirect" title="Direct free kick">free kick</a> in the team's 3–1 win over <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">FC Barcelona</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> On 21 January 2017, De Bruyne was involved in both of City's goals, as he netted once himself and also assisted <a href="/wiki/Leroy_San%C3%A9" title="Leroy Sané">Leroy Sané</a>'s, in a 2–2 home draw with <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a>; he was subsequently named <i>Man of the Match</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> On 19 March 2017, De Bruyne displayed an excellent performance in a 1–1 draw against <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a> at the <a href="/wiki/City_of_Manchester_Stadium" title="City of Manchester Stadium">Etihad Stadium</a>, where he set up a goal for <a href="/wiki/Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero" title="Sergio Agüero">Agüero</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup></p><div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:260px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Kevin_de_Bruyne_(36243870980).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/33/Kevin_de_Bruyne_%2836243870980%29.jpg/258px-Kevin_de_Bruyne_%2836243870980%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="258" height="171" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/33/Kevin_de_Bruyne_%2836243870980%29.jpg/387px-Kevin_de_Bruyne_%2836243870980%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/33/Kevin_de_Bruyne_%2836243870980%29.jpg/516px-Kevin_de_Bruyne_%2836243870980%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4912" data-file-height="3264" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Kevin_de_Bruyne_(36243870980).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>De Bruyne during a pre-season training session, in July 2017.</div></div></div>
<h4><span id="2017.E2.80.9318_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2017–18_season">2017–18 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kevin_De_Bruyne&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: 2017–18 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>De Bruyne set up both <a href="/wiki/Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero" title="Sergio Agüero">Agüero</a>'s and <a href="/wiki/Gabriel_Jesus" title="Gabriel Jesus">Gabriel Jesus</a>' goals, on 9 September 2017, in a 5–0 home victory over <a href="/wiki/FC_Liverpool" class="mw-redirect" title="FC Liverpool">Liverpool</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> On 16 September, De Bruyne assisted <a href="/wiki/Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero" title="Sergio Agüero">Agüero</a> for his first goal in an eventual 6–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Watford_F.C." title="Watford F.C.">Watford</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> On 26 September, De Bruyne scored his first goal of the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Manchester_City_F.C._season" title="2017–18 Manchester City F.C. season">2017–18 season</a> in a 2–0 win over <a href="/wiki/FC_Shakhtar_Donetsk" title="FC Shakhtar Donetsk">Shakhtar Donetsk</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> On 30 September 2017, he scored his first goal of the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Premier_League" title="2017–18 Premier League">2017–18 Premier League</a> season, as City beat his former club <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_FC" class="mw-redirect" title="Chelsea FC">Chelsea</a> with a 1–0 scoreline at <a href="/wiki/Stamford_Bridge_(stadium)" title="Stamford Bridge (stadium)">Stamford Bridge</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> On 14 October, De Bruyne provided two assists in a 7–2 win over <a href="/wiki/Stoke_City_F.C." title="Stoke City F.C.">Stoke City</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> On 5 November, De Bruyne scored in a 3–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> On 18 November, he scored in a 2–0 away win over <a href="/wiki/Leicester_City_F.C." title="Leicester City F.C.">Leicester City</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> On 29 November, he scored City's opener and assisted <a href="/wiki/Raheem_Sterling" title="Raheem Sterling">Sterling's</a> last-minute winner in a 2–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Southampton_F.C." title="Southampton F.C.">Southampton</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 13 December, De Bruyne scored in a 4–0 away win over <a href="/wiki/Swansea_City_A.F.C." title="Swansea City A.F.C.">Swansea City</a>, which extended their record run of consecutive top-flight wins to 15 games.<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup> On 16 December, he scored in a 4–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur_F.C." title="Tottenham Hotspur F.C.">Tottenham Hotspur</a>, with <a href="/wiki/Pep_Guardiola" title="Pep Guardiola">Pep Guardiola</a> saying that De Bruyne is "helping the club become a better institution".<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> On 27 December, De Bruyne provided an assist for Sterling's goal in a 1–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Newcastle_United_F.C." title="Newcastle United F.C.">Newcastle United</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> On 9 January, De Bruyne scored in a 2–1 win over Bristol City in the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_EFL_Cup#Semi-finals" title="2017–18 EFL Cup">first leg of the semi-finals</a> of the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_EFL_Cup" title="2017–18 EFL Cup">EFL Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> On 20 January, he provided an assist for <a href="/wiki/Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero" title="Sergio Agüero">Agüero's</a> first goal of the game (who scored a <a href="/wiki/Hat-trick" title="Hat-trick">hat-trick</a> in the game), in a 3–1 win over Newcastle United.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:254px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Manchester_United_v_Manchester_City,_10_December_2017_(20).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a0/Manchester_United_v_Manchester_City%2C_10_December_2017_%2820%29.jpg/252px-Manchester_United_v_Manchester_City%2C_10_December_2017_%2820%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="252" height="189" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a0/Manchester_United_v_Manchester_City%2C_10_December_2017_%2820%29.jpg/378px-Manchester_United_v_Manchester_City%2C_10_December_2017_%2820%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a0/Manchester_United_v_Manchester_City%2C_10_December_2017_%2820%29.jpg/504px-Manchester_United_v_Manchester_City%2C_10_December_2017_%2820%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2560" data-file-height="1920" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Manchester_United_v_Manchester_City,_10_December_2017_(20).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>De Bruyne during the <a href="/wiki/Manchester_derby" title="Manchester derby">Manchester derby</a> at <a href="/wiki/Old_Trafford" title="Old Trafford">Old Trafford</a>, on 10 December 2017, a match City won 2–1.</div></div></div>
<p>On 22 January 2018, De Bruyne signed a new long-term contract with the club, keeping him at the club until 2023.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-BBC_Sport_87-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC_Sport-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> On 23 January, he scored the winning goal in a 3–2 win over Bristol City in the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_EFL_Cup#Semi-finals" title="2017–18 EFL Cup">EFL Cup semi-final second leg</a>, which helped City advance to the <a href="/wiki/2018_EFL_Cup_Final" title="2018 EFL Cup Final">final</a>, having won the tie by an aggregate scoreline of 5–3.<sup id="cite_ref-BBC_Sport_87-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC_Sport-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> On 31 January, he scored and assisted in a 3–0 win over <a href="/wiki/West_Bromwich_Albion_F.C." title="West Bromwich Albion F.C.">West Bromwich Albion</a>, and was voted <a href="/wiki/BBC_Sport" title="BBC Sport">BBC</a> <i>Man of the Match</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-BBC_Sport_87-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-BBC_Sport-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> On 10 February, he provided three assists, two for <a href="/wiki/Sergio_Ag%C3%BCero" title="Sergio Agüero">Sergio Agüero</a> and one for <a href="/wiki/Raheem_Sterling" title="Raheem Sterling">Raheem Sterling</a>, in a 5–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Leicester_City_F.C." title="Leicester City F.C.">Leicester City</a>, taking his assists tally to 14.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup> On 25 February, he started in the <a href="/wiki/2018_EFL_Cup_Final" title="2018 EFL Cup Final">2018 EFL Cup Final</a> against <a href="/wiki/Arsenal_F.C." title="Arsenal F.C.">Arsenal</a>, and played the whole 90 minutes, with Manchester City winning 3–0 to obtain their first piece of silverware of the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Manchester_City_F.C._season" title="2017–18 Manchester City F.C. season">2017–18 season</a>, and their first trophy overall under <a href="/wiki/Pep_Guardiola" title="Pep Guardiola">Pep Guardiola</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 31 March 2018, he provided an assist for <a href="/wiki/Gabriel_Jesus" title="Gabriel Jesus">Gabriel Jesus</a> in a 3–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Everton_F.C." title="Everton F.C.">Everton</a>, ensuring that City would require only one more win to secure the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Premier_League" title="2017–18 Premier League">Premier League title</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup> On 22 April, he scored in a 5–0 win over Swansea City.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> On 13 May, on the final day of the season, De Bruyne assisted <a href="/wiki/Gabriel_Jesus" title="Gabriel Jesus">Gabriel Jesus</a>' winning goal in a 1–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Southampton_F.C." title="Southampton F.C.">Southampton</a>, which took champions City's total points tally to 100. De Bruyne was also voted as <a href="/wiki/BBC_Sport" title="BBC Sport">BBC</a> <i>Man of the Match</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup> For his 16 assists registered across the league season, De Bruyne won the inaugural <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_Playmaker_of_the_Season" title="Premier League Playmaker of the Season">Premier League Playmaker of the Season award</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup> He was also selected in the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Team_of_the_Year_(2010s)#Premier_League_9" title="PFA Team of the Year (2010s)">PFA Team of the Year</a>, and was also voted as <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C.#Player_of_the_Year" title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City Player of the Season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2018.E2.80.9319_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2018–19_season">2018–19 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kevin_De_Bruyne&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: 2018–19 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 15 August 2018, De Bruyne suffered a knee injury during a training session, with several news websites reporting that he could potentially not play for up to three months.<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> Two days later, Manchester City confirmed that he had suffered a lesion of the <a href="/wiki/Fibular_collateral_ligament" title="Fibular collateral ligament">lateral collateral ligament</a> in his right knee, with no surgery required, and that he was expected to not play for three months.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup> Soon after De Bruyne returned to action in October 2018, he once again suffered a knee ligament injury in the 4th round of the <a href="/wiki/EFL_Cup" title="EFL Cup">EFL Cup</a> against <a href="/wiki/Fulham_F.C." title="Fulham F.C.">Fulham</a>. The injury was expected to keep him out for 5–6 weeks<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup> but he resumed full training much earlier than expected after only 3 weeks out.<sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup> He came on as substitute in the <a href="/wiki/2019_FA_Cup_Final" title="2019 FA Cup Final">FA Cup final</a> against <a href="/wiki/Watford_F.C." title="Watford F.C.">Watford</a>, scoring the third goal and assisting two more, as City won the first-ever domestic treble in English men's football.<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:0_108-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup> His performances meant he was named <i>Man of the Match</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_108-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2019.E2.80.9320_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2019–20_season">2019–20 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kevin_De_Bruyne&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: 2019–20 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 30 November 2019, De Bruyne scored a half volley in a 2–2 draw against Newcastle in the league, that strike was later voted as <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_Goal_of_the_Month" title="Premier League Goal of the Month">Premier League Goal of the Month</a> for November.<sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup> On 15 December 2019, he scored a brace in a 3–0 <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Premier_League" title="2019–20 Premier League">Premier League</a> win over Arsenal at the Emirates.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>De Bruyne scored his 50th City goal in all competitions on 26 February 2020 in their 2–1 victory, coming from behind, over <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_CF" title="Real Madrid CF">Real Madrid</a> in their Champions League <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_UEFA_Champions_League#Round_of_16" title="2019–20 UEFA Champions League">Round of 16</a> clash.<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the final Premier League match of the season, City beat <a href="/wiki/Norwich_City_F.C." title="Norwich City F.C.">Norwich City</a> 5–0 at home. De Bruyne scored two goals and registered his 20th league assist, which equalled <a href="/wiki/Thierry_Henry" title="Thierry Henry">Thierry Henry</a>'s record for the most assists in a season, and also won his second <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_Playmaker_of_the_Season" title="Premier League Playmaker of the Season">Playmaker of the Season</a> award.<sup id="cite_ref-:1_113-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup> In addition he became the first player in history to reach 20 assists in a single season in two of Europe's top five leagues.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup> His long range curler in that game also won him <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_Goal_of_the_Month" title="Premier League Goal of the Month">Premier League Goal of the Month</a> for the second time in the season.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At the end of the season he was awarded the <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_Player_of_the_Season" title="Premier League Player of the Season">Premier League Player of the Season</a> after scoring 13 goals, providing 20 assists and creating 104 chances from open play, the most for a player in any of Europe's top five leagues since 2006.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>He was also named in the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Team_of_the_Year_(2010s)" title="PFA Team of the Year (2010s)">PFA Team of the Year</a> and won the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Players%27_Player_of_the_Year" title="PFA Players&#39; Player of the Year">PFA Player of the Year</a> award, becoming the first ever Manchester City player to win it.<sup id="cite_ref-:2_119-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:2-119">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2020.E2.80.9321_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2020–21_season">2020–21 season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kevin_De_Bruyne&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: 2020–21 season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 21 September 2020, De Bruyne scored and assisted in a 3–1 away win over <a href="/wiki/Wolverhampton_Wanderers_F.C." title="Wolverhampton Wanderers F.C.">Wolves</a> in City's first game of the season.<sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup> With the crucial visit of the Premier League champions, Liverpool, De Bruyne assisted Gabriel Jesus' equalizer before winning a penalty, which he subsequently fired wide. The game ended in a 1–1 draw. <sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kevin_De_Bruyne&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:258px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Vincent_Kompany_Simon_Mignolet_Kevin_De_Bruyne_vs_USA.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Vincent_Kompany_Simon_Mignolet_Kevin_De_Bruyne_vs_USA.jpg/256px-Vincent_Kompany_Simon_Mignolet_Kevin_De_Bruyne_vs_USA.jpg" decoding="async" width="256" height="161" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Vincent_Kompany_Simon_Mignolet_Kevin_De_Bruyne_vs_USA.jpg/384px-Vincent_Kompany_Simon_Mignolet_Kevin_De_Bruyne_vs_USA.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1b/Vincent_Kompany_Simon_Mignolet_Kevin_De_Bruyne_vs_USA.jpg/512px-Vincent_Kompany_Simon_Mignolet_Kevin_De_Bruyne_vs_USA.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3504" data-file-height="2208" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Vincent_Kompany_Simon_Mignolet_Kevin_De_Bruyne_vs_USA.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>De Bruyne <i>(right)</i> lining up for Belgium in 2013, alongside <a href="/wiki/Vincent_Kompany" title="Vincent Kompany">Vincent Kompany</a> and <a href="/wiki/Simon_Mignolet" title="Simon Mignolet">Simon Mignolet</a>.</div></div></div>
<p>De Bruyne was capped by <a href="/wiki/Belgium_national_football_team" title="Belgium national football team">Belgium</a> at <a href="/wiki/Belgium_national_under-18_football_team" title="Belgium national under-18 football team">under-18</a>, <a href="/wiki/Belgium_national_under-19_football_team" title="Belgium national under-19 football team">under-19</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Belgium_national_under-21_football_team" title="Belgium national under-21 football team">under-21</a> level. He made his debut for the <a href="/wiki/Belgium_national_football_team" title="Belgium national football team">Belgian senior team</a> on 11 August 2010 in an international friendly against <a href="/wiki/Finland_national_football_team" title="Finland national football team">Finland</a> in <a href="/wiki/Turku" title="Turku">Turku</a>; the game ended in a 1–0 loss for Belgium.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Before making his full debut for Belgium's senior side, De Bruyne was eligible to play for <a href="/wiki/Burundi_national_football_team" title="Burundi national football team">Burundi</a>, his mother's birthplace.<sup id="cite_ref-fightforchance_123-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-fightforchance-123">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>De Bruyne became a regular member of Belgium's team during the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_-_UEFA_Group_A" class="mw-redirect" title="2014 FIFA World Cup qualification - UEFA Group A">2014 FIFA World Cup qualification</a> campaign, where he scored four goals as the Red Devils qualified for their first major tournament in 12 years.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 13 May 2014, he was named in Belgium's squad for the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2014 FIFA World Cup">2014 FIFA World Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-125" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-125">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup> In their first game of the tournament, against <a href="/wiki/Algeria_national_football_team" title="Algeria national football team">Algeria</a> in <a href="/wiki/Belo_Horizonte" title="Belo Horizonte">Belo Horizonte</a>, De Bruyne assisted <a href="/wiki/Marouane_Fellaini" title="Marouane Fellaini">Marouane Fellaini</a>'s equaliser<sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup> and was named <a href="/wiki/Man_of_the_match" class="mw-redirect" title="Man of the match">man of the match</a> by <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/2014_FIFA_World_Cup_round_of_16" class="mw-redirect" title="2014 FIFA World Cup round of 16">round of 16</a>, De Bruyne scored Belgium's opening goal in the third minute of <a href="/wiki/Overtime#Association_football" title="Overtime">extra time</a> as they defeated the <a href="/wiki/United_States_men%27s_national_soccer_team" title="United States men&#39;s national soccer team">United States</a> 2–1.<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:258px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Kevin_De_Bruyne_celebrating_Belgium%27s_2%E2%80%931_win_over_Brazil.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Kevin_De_Bruyne_celebrating_Belgium%27s_2%E2%80%931_win_over_Brazil.jpg/256px-Kevin_De_Bruyne_celebrating_Belgium%27s_2%E2%80%931_win_over_Brazil.jpg" decoding="async" width="256" height="176" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Kevin_De_Bruyne_celebrating_Belgium%27s_2%E2%80%931_win_over_Brazil.jpg/384px-Kevin_De_Bruyne_celebrating_Belgium%27s_2%E2%80%931_win_over_Brazil.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/69/Kevin_De_Bruyne_celebrating_Belgium%27s_2%E2%80%931_win_over_Brazil.jpg/512px-Kevin_De_Bruyne_celebrating_Belgium%27s_2%E2%80%931_win_over_Brazil.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1341" data-file-height="921" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Kevin_De_Bruyne_celebrating_Belgium%27s_2%E2%80%931_win_over_Brazil.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>De Bruyne celebrating Belgium's 2–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil</a>, on 6 July 2018.</div></div></div>
<p>On 10 October 2014, De Bruyne scored twice in a 6–0 rout of <a href="/wiki/Andorra_national_football_team" title="Andorra national football team">Andorra</a> in <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016_qualifying" title="UEFA Euro 2016 qualifying">UEFA Euro 2016 qualifying</a>, equaling the team's record victory in a European qualifier set in 1986.<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup> On 3 September 2015, De Bruyne scored in a 3–1 win over Bosnia and Herzegovina.<sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup> On 10 October 2015, De Bruyne scored in a 4–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Andorra_national_football_team" title="Andorra national football team">Andorra</a>, which secured Belgium's place at the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">UEFA Euro 2016 finals</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup> Three days later, he scored in a 3–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Israel_national_football_team" title="Israel national football team">Israel</a>, securing Belgium <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016_qualifying_Group_B" title="UEFA Euro 2016 qualifying Group B">top-spot in the group</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup>
On 31 May 2016, De Bruyne was selected for Belgium's final 23-man <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016_squads#Belgium" title="UEFA Euro 2016 squads">squad</a> for <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">UEFA Euro 2016</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup> On 18 June 2016, De Bruyne was praised for his performance in Belgium's 3–0 win over the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland_national_football_team" title="Republic of Ireland national football team">Republic of Ireland</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup> On 26 June 2016, De Bruyne was voted <a href="/wiki/BBC_Sport" title="BBC Sport">BBC</a> <i>Man of the Match</i> for his performance in a 4–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Hungary_national_football_team" title="Hungary national football team">Hungary</a> in the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016#Round_of_16" title="UEFA Euro 2016">round of sixteen</a>, where he provided two assists.<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>De Bruyne was selected for Belgium's final 23-man <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_squads#Belgium" title="2018 FIFA World Cup squads">squad</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-138" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-138">&#91;138&#93;</a></sup> On 18 June, in the opening game against debutants <a href="/wiki/Panama_national_football_team" title="Panama national football team">Panama</a>, De Bruyne provided an assist for <a href="/wiki/Romelu_Lukaku" title="Romelu Lukaku">Romelu Lukaku</a> in an eventual 3–0 win.<sup id="cite_ref-139" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-139">&#91;139&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-140" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-140">&#91;140&#93;</a></sup> On 6 July, he scored the second goal of the match in a 2–1 <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_knockout_stage#Brazil_vs_Belgium" title="2018 FIFA World Cup knockout stage">quarter-final</a> victory over <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil</a> and was named the <a href="/wiki/Player_of_the_match" title="Player of the match">Man of the Match</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-141" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-141">&#91;141&#93;</a></sup> In the semi-finals, Belgium were defeated 1–0 by eventual champions <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-142" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-142">&#91;142&#93;</a></sup> On 14 July, Belgium defeated <a href="/wiki/England_national_football_team" title="England national football team">England</a> 2–0 in the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup#Third_place_play-off" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">third-place play-off</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-143" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-143">&#91;143&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kevin_De_Bruyne&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>De Bruyne is widely regarded as one of the best players in the world,<sup id="cite_ref-144" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-144">&#91;144&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-145" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-145">&#91;145&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-146" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-146">&#91;146&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-147" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-147">&#91;147&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-148" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-148">&#91;148&#93;</a></sup> and he has often been described as a "complete" footballer.<sup id="cite_ref-149" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-149">&#91;149&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-150" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-150">&#91;150&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-151" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-151">&#91;151&#93;</a></sup> Considered to be a versatile and highly talented player in the media, he plays mainly as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Central_midfielder" title="Midfielder">central</a> or an <a href="/wiki/Attacking_midfielder" class="mw-redirect" title="Attacking midfielder">attacking midfielder</a> but can also operate in several other positions, and has been used as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Winger" title="Midfielder">winger</a> or <a href="/wiki/Second_striker" class="mw-redirect" title="Second striker">second striker</a>; he has even been deployed in a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Deep-lying_playmaker" title="Midfielder">deeper creative midfield position</a>, or even in a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Box-to-box_midfielder" title="Midfielder">box-to-box role</a> on occasion. He is often described by pundits as one of the best and most complete modern day <a href="/wiki/Playmaker" title="Playmaker">advanced playmakers</a>, due to his technique, skill, athleticism, work-rate off the ball, vision, <a href="/wiki/Cross_(football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Cross (football)">crossing</a> accuracy, wide range of passing, and powerful long-range shooting ability with either foot.<sup id="cite_ref-152" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-152">&#91;152&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-153" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-153">&#91;153&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-154" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-154">&#91;154&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-155" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-155">&#91;155&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-156" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-156">&#91;156&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-157" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-157">&#91;157&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-158" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-158">&#91;158&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Although he is not blessed with significant physical strength, pace, or ability in the air,<sup id="cite_ref-Generazione_di_Fenomeni_159-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Generazione_di_Fenomeni-159">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup> he is a quick and elegant player on the ball, with good <a href="/wiki/Dribbling#Association_football" title="Dribbling">dribbling</a> skills, while his positional sense, tactical intelligence, movement, direct style of play, and ability to run at defences when in possession also enable him to take advantage of spaces in the opposition's defence, and subsequently create chances and goalscoring opportunities for himself or his teammates, making him a dangerous offensive threat on counter-attacks.<sup id="cite_ref-Generazione_di_Fenomeni_159-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Generazione_di_Fenomeni-159">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-160" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-160">&#91;160&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-161" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-161">&#91;161&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-162" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-162">&#91;162&#93;</a></sup> In addition to his creative abilities,<sup id="cite_ref-Generazione_di_Fenomeni_159-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Generazione_di_Fenomeni-159">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup> he is also capable of scoring goals by making late runs off the ball from behind into the penalty area,<sup id="cite_ref-163" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-163">&#91;163&#93;</a></sup> and is an accurate <a href="/wiki/Direct_free_kick" class="mw-redirect" title="Direct free kick">set-piece</a> taker.<sup id="cite_ref-Generazione_di_Fenomeni_159-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Generazione_di_Fenomeni-159">&#91;159&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-164" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-164">&#91;164&#93;</a></sup> De Bruyne was ranked the fourth-best footballer in the world by <i><a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">The Guardian</a></i> in 2017<sup id="cite_ref-165" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-165">&#91;165&#93;</a></sup> and the twelfth-best in 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-166" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-166">&#91;166&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kevin_De_Bruyne&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:162px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Kevin_De_Bruyne_at_Samsung.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/Kevin_De_Bruyne_at_Samsung.jpg/160px-Kevin_De_Bruyne_at_Samsung.jpg" decoding="async" width="160" height="240" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/Kevin_De_Bruyne_at_Samsung.jpg/240px-Kevin_De_Bruyne_at_Samsung.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/Kevin_De_Bruyne_at_Samsung.jpg/320px-Kevin_De_Bruyne_at_Samsung.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3648" data-file-height="5472" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Kevin_De_Bruyne_at_Samsung.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>De Bruyne in the Samsung Showroom, during the Red Devils visit.</div></div></div>
<p>De Bruyne's mother is Belgian,<sup id="cite_ref-167" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-167">&#91;167&#93;</a></sup> born in <a href="/wiki/Burundi" title="Burundi">Burundi</a> and has also lived in the <a href="/wiki/Ivory_Coast" title="Ivory Coast">Ivory Coast</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-168" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-168">&#91;168&#93;</a></sup> His hometown <a href="/wiki/Drongen" title="Drongen">Drongen</a>, a submunicipality of the city of <a href="/wiki/Ghent" title="Ghent">Ghent</a>, is situated in <a href="/wiki/Flanders" title="Flanders">Flanders</a>, the Dutch-speaking part of Belgium.<sup id="cite_ref-169" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-169">&#91;169&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-170" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-170">&#91;170&#93;</a></sup> Aside from his mother tongue <a href="/wiki/Dutch_language" title="Dutch language">Dutch</a>, De Bruyne also speaks <a href="/wiki/French_language" title="French language">French</a>, <a href="/wiki/English_language" title="English language">English</a> and <a href="/wiki/German_language" title="German language">German</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-171" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-171">&#91;171&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-172" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-172">&#91;172&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Since 2014, De Bruyne has been in a relationship with Michèle Lacroix,<sup id="cite_ref-173" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-173">&#91;173&#93;</a></sup> who announced on 28 September 2015 that she was pregnant with the couple's son.<sup id="cite_ref-174" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-174">&#91;174&#93;</a></sup> Mason Milian De Bruyne was born on 10 March 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-175" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-175">&#91;175&#93;</a></sup> Their second son, Rome De Bruyne, was born on 31 October 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-176" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-176">&#91;176&#93;</a></sup> De Bruyne and Lacroix married in June 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-177" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-177">&#91;177&#93;</a></sup> In April 2020, it was announced that they were expecting their third child,<sup id="cite_ref-178" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-178">&#91;178&#93;</a></sup> who was later born in September 2020, to be their first daughter named Suri De Bruyne.<sup id="cite_ref-179" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-179">&#91;179&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>His autobiography, entitled <i>Keep It Simple</i>, was published by Borgerhoff &amp; Lamberigts in October 2014.<sup id="cite_ref-northcroft_180-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-northcroft-180">&#91;180&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>De Bruyne was an ambassador for the 2014 <a href="/wiki/Special_Olympics" title="Special Olympics">Special Olympics</a>, which took place in <a href="/wiki/Antwerp" title="Antwerp">Antwerp</a> and was involved in a controversial advertisement campaign, via his personal <a href="/wiki/Instagram" title="Instagram">Instagram</a> account. Employing the slogan (in <a href="/wiki/Dutch_language" title="Dutch language">Dutch</a>): "Would you still be my fan if I looked like this?", De Bruyne was depicted resembling a person with <a href="/wiki/Down_syndrome" title="Down syndrome">Down syndrome</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-181" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-181">&#91;181&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kevin_De_Bruyne&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Career statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Kevin_De_Bruyne&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div style=""><ol class="references" style="list-style-type:disc;">
<li id="cnote_N1"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#ref_N1_1">^</a></b></span> <div style="display:inline;" class="reference-text">While several sources indicate that De Bruyne recorded 21 assists during the season, this number has been disputed and in 2020, the official Bundesliga website credited De Bruyne with 19 assists.<sup id="cite_ref-249" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-249">&#91;241&#93;</a></sup></div></li>
<li id="cnote_N2"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#ref_N2_1">^</a></b></span> <div style="display:inline;" class="reference-text">De Bruyne caps against <a href="/wiki/Romania_national_football_team" title="Romania national football team">Romania</a> on 14 November 2012, against <a href="/wiki/Luxembourg_national_football_team" title="Luxembourg national football team">Luxembourg</a> (included his one goal) on 26 May 2014 and against <a href="/wiki/Czech_national_football_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Czech national football team">Czech Republic</a> on 5 June 2017 were counted by <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.belgianfootball.be/nl/alle-rode-duivels">RBFA</a> but not officially recognised by <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a> due to an excessive number of <a href="/wiki/Substitute_(association_football)" title="Substitute (association football)">substitutions</a> according to the <a href="/wiki/Laws_of_the_Game_(association_football)" title="Laws of the Game (association football)">Laws of the Game</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-FArules_250-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FArules-250">&#91;242&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-251" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-251">&#91;243&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-252" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-252">&#91;244&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-253" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-253">&#91;245&#93;</a></sup></div></li>
</ol></div>
